comments
395 -> sulfurtransferase TusD -> Part of a sulfur-relay system required for 2-thiolation of 5-methylaminomethyl-2-thiouridine (mnm5s2U) at tRNA wobble positions. Accepts sulfur from TusA and transfers it in turn to TusE. Not likely to be related to antibacterial resistance.
